πρᾶος
930a

<div2 id="crosspra=os" orig_id="n86187" key="pra=os" type="main" opt="n"><head extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n" orth_orig="πρᾶος">πρᾶος</head>, <itype lang="greek" opt="n">ον</itype>, also <orth extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n">πρᾱΰς</orth>, <gramGrp opt="n"><gram type="dialect" opt="n">Ion.</gram></gramGrp> <orth extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n">πρηΰς</orth>, <itype lang="greek" opt="n">εῖα</itype>, <itype lang="greek">ΰ</itype>:—<orth extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n">πρᾶος</orth> supplies sg. in <gramGrp opt="n"><gram type="dialect" opt="n">Att.</gram></gramGrp>, Trag., and Com., exc. that the fem. is always <foreign lang="greek">πραεῖα </foreign> (<foreign lang="greek">πρᾶος</foreign> as fem. only in <bibl n="Perseus:abo:tlg,0007,080:168d"><author>Plu.</author> <title>[Superst.]</title> 2.168d</bibl>); but sg. <orth extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n">πραΰς</orth>, <gramGrp opt="n"><gram type="dialect" opt="n">Ion.</gram></gramGrp> <orth extent="full" lang="greek" opt="n">πρηΰς</orth>, is used in <gramGrp opt="n"><gram type="dialect" opt="n">Ep.</gram></gramGrp> and Lyr.
